Welcome to Jamagrasha

If you’re looking for a unique gift online, you’ve come to the right place. Jamagrasha is home to a selection of keychains, jewelry boxes and special gifts that would be perfect for all those who love uniqueness and beauty, just with a smaller price tag. Offering a collection of keychains, brooches, small jewelry boxes and decorative gift boxes, Jamagrasha combines functionality and beauty. Designed with quality metal alloy and rhinestones, our gifts bring that wonderful touch of sparkle and dazzle through their unique designs, shapes and colors.
